import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S

def _launch():
    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
INPUT0_SHAPE = (8, 64, 512, 1024)
OUTPUT_SHAPE = (8, 128, 510, 1022)
WEIGHT_SHAPE = (128, 64, 3, 3)

@substrate.jit
def fused_kernel(X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 1024), S.f32), W: S.Tensor((128, 64, 3, 3), S.f32), Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 510, 1022), S.f32)):
    for n in S.range(8):
        for oc in S.range(128):
            for o0 in S.range(510):
                for o1 in S.range(1022):
                    acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
                    g = oc // 128
                    ic_base = g * 64
                    for ic_local in S.range(64):
                        ic = ic_base + ic_local
                        for k0 in S.range(3):
                            for k1 in S.range(3):
                                i0 = o0 * 1 - 0 + k0 * 1
                                i1 = o1 * 1 - 0 + k1 * 1
                                if (i0 >= 0 and i0 < 512) and (i1 >= 0 and i1 < 1024):
                                    acc += S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.f32) * S.convert(W[oc, ic_local, k0, k1], S.f32)
                    Y[n, oc, o0, o1] = acc

class ModelNew(nn.Module):

    def __init__(self, in_channels: int, out_channels: int, kernel_size: int, stride: int = 1, padding: int = 0, dilation: int = 1, groups: int = 1, bias: bool = False):
            super(ModelNew, self).__init__()
            self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(in_channels, out_channels, (kernel_size, kernel_size), stride=stride, padding=padding, dilation=dilation, groups=groups, bias=bias)

    def forward(self, x):
        if tuple(x.shape) != (8, 64, 512, 1024) or x.dtype != torch.float32:
            raise RuntimeError('This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.')
        x0 = x.contiguous()
        w = self.conv2d.weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        y = torch.empty((8, 128, 510, 1022), device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)
        fused_kernel[_launch](x0, w, y)
        return y

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest
import sys

import torch
import torch.nn.functional as F

# Import the optimized kernel - PATH TO p56
sys.path.insert(0, "/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p83/optimization_rounds_claude/round2")
from output_model_new import ModelNew, BATCH_SIZE, IN_CHANNELS, IN_H, IN_W, OUT_CHANNELS, KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W, OUT_H, OUT_W


class TestMFMAConv2D(unittest.TestCase):
    """Test MFMA-optimized Conv2D kernel."""

    def setUp(self):
        """Set up test fixtures before each test method."""
        torch.manual_seed(0)
        self.rtol = 1e-2
        self.atol = 0.1  # Tolerance for bf16 precision

    def test_mfma_conv2d_benchmark_shape(self):
        """Test MFMA Conv2D for the benchmark shapes."""
        if not torch.cuda.is_available():
            self.skipTest("CUDA is not available.")
        if not hasattr(torch.version, "hip") or torch.version.hip is None:
            self.skipTest("HIP is not available.")

        # Create model with the kernel's expected parameters
        # For p56: in_channels=64, out_channels=128, kernel_size=(5, 7), groups=1
        model = ModelNew(
            in_channels=IN_CHANNELS,
            out_channels=OUT_CHANNELS,
            kernel_size=(KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W),
            stride=(1, 1),
            padding=(0, 0),
            bias=False
        ).cuda()

        # Create input with the specific shape the kernel expects
        x = torch.randn((BATCH_SIZE, IN_CHANNELS, IN_H, IN_W), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")

        # Run optimized kernel
        actual = model(x)

        # Compute expected result using PyTorch (depthwise conv2d with groups=IN_CHANNELS)
        weight = model.conv2d.weight.to(dtype=torch.float32)
        expected = F.conv2d(x, weight, stride=1, padding=0, groups=IN_CHANNELS)

        actual_cpu = actual.cpu().to(torch.float32)
        expected_cpu = expected.cpu()

        max_diff = torch.max(torch.abs(actual_cpu - expected_cpu)).item()
        mean_diff = torch.mean(torch.abs(actual_cpu - expected_cpu)).item()

        print(f"Max absolute difference: {max_diff}")
        print(f"Mean absolute difference: {mean_diff}")
        print(f"Actual shape: {actual.shape}")
        print(f"Expected shape: {expected.shape}")

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.allclose(actual_cpu, expected_cpu, rtol=self.rtol, atol=self.atol),
            msg=f"MFMA Conv2D results do not match.\n"
                f"Max absolute difference: {max_diff}\n"
                f"Mean absolute difference: {mean_diff}"
        )

    def test_mfma_conv2d_output_shape(self):
        """Test that output shape is correct."""
        if not torch.cuda.is_available():
            self.skipTest("CUDA is not available.")

        model = ModelNew(
            in_channels=IN_CHANNELS,
            out_channels=OUT_CHANNELS,
            kernel_size=(KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W),
            stride=(1, 1),
            padding=(0, 0),
            bias=False
        ).cuda()
        x = torch.randn((BATCH_SIZE, IN_CHANNELS, IN_H, IN_W), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")

        output = model(x)

        # Expected output matches kernel constants
        expected_shape = (BATCH_SIZE, OUT_CHANNELS, OUT_H, OUT_W)
        self.assertEqual(output.shape, expected_shape,
                         f"Output shape mismatch: got {output.shape}, expected {expected_shape}")


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main(verbosity=2)

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
Conv2D benchmark for AMDGPU using MFMA-tiled Split-K conv kernel.

Benchmarks the 3x3 conv2d kernel with Split-K reduction.
"""
import argparse
import sys

import torch
import torch.nn.functional as F

# Import the optimized kernel
sys.path.insert(0, "/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p83/optimization_rounds_claude/round2")
from output_model_new import ModelNew, BATCH_SIZE, IN_CHANNELS, IN_H, IN_W, OUT_CHANNELS, KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W, OUT_H, OUT_W


def _ensure_rocm_available(label):
    """Check that ROCm/HIP is available."""
    if not torch.cuda.is_available():
        raise RuntimeError("CUDA is not available.")
    if not hasattr(torch.version, "hip") or torch.version.hip is None:
        raise RuntimeError(f"HIP is not available; {label} benchmark requires ROCm.")


def run_conv2d_benchmark(
    warmup,
    repeat,
    validate,
):
    """
    Run conv2d benchmark with 3x3 kernel and Split-K reduction.

    Args:
        warmup: Number of warmup iterations
        repeat: Number of benchmark repeats
        validate: Whether to validate output correctness
    """
    _ensure_rocm_available("conv2d_mfma_splitk")

    # Fixed configuration for this kernel
    batch_size = BATCH_SIZE
    in_channels = IN_CHANNELS
    kernel_h = KERNEL_H
    kernel_w = KERNEL_W
    in_h = IN_H
    in_w = IN_W

    stride_h = stride_w = 1
    dilation = 1
    padding = 0

    out_h = OUT_H
    out_w = OUT_W
    out_channels = OUT_CHANNELS

    # Create ModelNew instance
    model = ModelNew(
        in_channels=in_channels,
        out_channels=out_channels,
        kernel_size=kernel_h,
        bias=False,
    ).cuda()

    # Create input tensor (float32 as required by ModelNew)
    input = torch.randn((batch_size, in_channels, in_h, in_w), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")

    print(f"Note: This benchmark uses MFMA-tiled {kernel_h}x{kernel_w} conv2d kernel with Split-K (SPLIT_K_SLICES=2).")
    print(f"Grid: batch={batch_size} in_channels={in_channels} out_channels={out_channels} "
          f"kernel=({kernel_h},{kernel_w}) in=({in_h},{in_w}) out=({out_h},{out_w})")

    for _ in range(warmup):
        model(input)
    torch.cuda.synchronize()

    start_evt = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
    end_evt = torch.cuda.Event(enable_timing=True)
    start_evt.record()
    for _ in range(repeat):
        model(input)
    end_evt.record()
    torch.cuda.synchronize()

    elapsed_ms = start_evt.elapsed_time(end_evt)
    elapsed = elapsed_ms * 1.0e-3 / repeat

    # Compute FLOPs: for each output element, multiply by kernel and accumulate
    flops_per_output = in_channels * kernel_h * kernel_w * 2  # mul + add
    total_flops = batch_size * out_channels * out_h * out_w * flops_per_output
    tflops = total_flops / elapsed / 1.0e12

    input_bytes = batch_size * in_channels * in_h * in_w * 4  # f32 = 4 bytes
    weight_bytes = out_channels * in_channels * kernel_h * kernel_w * 2  # bf16 = 2 bytes
    output_bytes = batch_size * out_channels * out_h * out_w * 4  # f32 = 4 bytes
    bytes_moved = input_bytes + weight_bytes + output_bytes
    bandwidth = bytes_moved / elapsed / 1.0e9

    print(
        f"batch={batch_size} in_channels={in_channels} out_channels={out_channels} "
        f"kernel=({kernel_h},{kernel_w}) in=({in_h},{in_w}) out=({out_h},{out_w}) "
        f"time_ms={elapsed * 1.0e3:.4f} tflops={tflops:.3f} bandwidth_gbs={bandwidth:.3f}"
    )

    if validate:
        x_f32 = input
        w_f32 = model.conv2d.weight.to(torch.float32)
        expected = torch.nn.functional.conv2d(x_f32, w_f32, stride=(stride_h, stride_w), padding=(padding, padding), dilation=(dilation, dilation), groups=IN_CHANNELS)
        actual = model(input).to(torch.float32)
        max_abs = torch.max(torch.abs(actual - expected)).item()
        # Use tolerance appropriate for bf16 precision (atol=0.1)
        if not torch.allclose(actual, expected, rtol=1e-2, atol=0.1):
            raise AssertionError(f"Validation failed (max abs diff {max_abs}).")
        print(f"validation=max_abs_diff:{max_abs:.6f}")


def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(
        description="AMDGPU Conv2D benchmark (MFMA-tiled Split-K conv)"
    )
    parser.add_argument("--warmup", type=int, default=1, help="Number of warmup iterations")
    parser.add_argument("--repeat", type=int, default=10, help="Number of benchmark repeats")
    parser.add_argument("--validate", action="store_true", default=False, help="Validate output correctness")
    args = parser.parse_args()

    run_conv2d_benchmark(
        warmup=args.warmup,
        repeat=args.repeat,
        validate=args.validate,
    )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()

/workspace/substrate/docs/skills/draft-substrate-program/SKILL.md:8:Substrate DSL is a tile-based DSL to write performant GPU kernels. It is syntacially close to PyCuTe / Triton. Substrate is not a block-based DSL, it exposes low-level constructs like `__syncthreads()`, and MFMA, buffer load intrinsics in the language to enable full utiliziations of the hardware features. The repo contains the implementation of the language (both C++ and Python infrastructure).

class dtype:
    SINT_TYPES = ["i8", "i16", "i32", "i64"]
    UINT_TYPES = ["u1", "u8", "u16", "u32", "u64"]
    FP_TYPES = ["fp16", "bf16", "fp32", "fp64"]
    STANDARD_FP_TYPES = ["fp16", "bf16", "fp32", "fp64"]
    OTHER_TYPES = ["void"]

    def __init__(self, name):
        self.name = name
        assert name in dtype.SINT_TYPES + dtype.UINT_TYPES + dtype.FP_TYPES + dtype.OTHER_TYPES, name


# scalar types
# Signed integer types
i8 = dtype("i8")
i16 = dtype("i16")
i32 = dtype("i32")
i64 = dtype("i64")

# Unsigned integer types
u1 = dtype("u1")
u8 = dtype("u8")
u16 = dtype("u16")
u32 = dtype("u32")
u64 = dtype("u64")

# Floating-point types
f16 = dtype("fp16")
bf16 = dtype("bf16")
f32 = dtype("fp32")
f64 = dtype("fp64")

# Other types
void = dtype("void")


dynamic = -1


class Tensor:
    """Multi-dimensional tensor type."""

    def __init__(self, shape, element_ty):
        self.shape = shape
        self.element_ty = element_ty


class pointer_type:
    def __init__(self, element_ty):
        self.element_ty = element_ty


Pointer = pointer_type


class constexpr_type:
    def __init__(self, value):
        self.value = value

    def __eq__(self, other):
        return isinstance(other, constexpr_type) and self.value == other.value

    def __repr__(self) -> str:
        return f"constexpr_type[{self.value}]"


class constexpr:
    """
    This class is used to store a value that is known at compile-time.
    """

    def __init__(self, value):
        while isinstance(value, constexpr):
            value = value.value
        self.value = value
        self.type = constexpr_type(value)

    def __repr__(self) -> str:
        return f"constexpr[{self.value}]"

    def __hash__(self):
        return hash((self.value, self.type))

/bin/bash -lc "sed -n '1,220p' /workspace/substrate/test/primitives/jit/test_num_warps.py" in /workspace/kernel_benchmark

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import _substrate_bindings as _C
import substrate
import substrate.language as S

from substrate.compiler import code_generator as cg
from substrate.compiler.code_generator import (
    _build_import_module,
    _collect_jit_dependencies,
    _get_function_def,
)
from substrate.compiler.compiler import ASTSource


@substrate.jit
def kernel_with_num_warps(
    x: S.Tensor((1,), S.i32),
    BLOCK_SIZE: S.constexpr,
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    if tid < BLOCK_SIZE:
        x[tid] = x[tid]


class TestNumWarps(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_amdgpu_llvm_ir_overrides_flat_workgroup_size_when_num_warps_set(self):
        src = ASTSource(
            kernel_with_num_warps,
            {"x": "*i32", "BLOCK_SIZE": "constexpr"},
            constexprs={"BLOCK_SIZE": {"type": "i32", "value": 16}},
        )
        constexprs_json = cg._serialize_constexprs(src)

        generator = _C.MLIRGenerator()
        import_module = _build_import_module(
            [kernel_with_num_warps, *_collect_jit_dependencies(kernel_with_num_warps)]
        )
        generator.generate_from_python_ast(import_module)
        generator.visit_function_def(
            _get_function_def(kernel_with_num_warps.parse()), constexprs_json, "kernel"
        )

        llvm_ir = generator.get_llvm_ir("amdgcn-amd-amdhsa", "gfx90a", 2, 3)
        self.assertIn('"amdgpu-flat-work-group-size"="1,192"', llvm_ir)


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

/bin/bash -lc "sed -n '760,860p' /workspace/substrate/python/substrate/runtime/jit.py" in /workspace/kernel_benchmark
 succeeded in 0ms:
            if k not in options.__dict__ and k not in sigkeys:
                raise KeyError("Keyword argument %s was specified but unrecognised" % k)
        # constexprs - now with name, type, and value
        constexpr_paths = find_paths_if(sigvals, lambda _, val: val == "constexpr")
        constexprs = {}
        for path in constexpr_paths:
            param_idx = path[0]
            param_name = self.arg_names[param_idx]
            value = get_iterable_path(list(bound_args.values()), path)
            # Unwrap constexpr wrapper if present
            if hasattr(value, "value"):
                value = value.value
            constexpr_type = self._infer_constexpr_type(value)
            constexprs[param_name] = {"type": constexpr_type, "value": value}
        global_constexprs = self._collect_global_constexprs(constexprs.keys())
        # attributes
        attrs = None

        return options, signature, constexprs, global_constexprs, attrs

    def run(self, dims, *args, **kwargs):
        # parse options
        device = driver.active.get_current_device()
        stream = driver.active.get_current_stream(device)

        kernel_cache, kernel_key_cache, target, backend, binder = self.device_caches[device]
        # specialization is list[tuple[str, Any]], where first element of tuple is
        # the type and the second parameter is the 'specialization' value.
        bound_args, specialization, options = binder(*args, **kwargs)

        grid, block = dims()

        options, signature, constexprs, global_constexprs, attrs = self._pack_args(
            backend, kwargs, bound_args, specialization, options
        )

        key = compute_cache_key(kernel_key_cache, specialization, options)
        kernel = kernel_cache.get(key, None)

        # Kernel is not cached; we have to compile.
        if kernel is None:
            options, signature, constexprs, global_constexprs, attrs = self._pack_args(
                backend, kwargs, bound_args, specialization, options
            )

            kernel = self._do_compile(
                key, signature, device, constexprs, global_constexprs, options, attrs
            )
            if kernel is None:
                raise RuntimeError(f"Kernel compilation failed for {self.__name__}")

        # TODO: support bound args so that args / kwargs work
        kernel.run(
            grid[0],
            grid[1],
            grid[2],
            block[0],
            block[1],
            block[2],
            stream,
            kernel.function,
            *bound_args.values(),
        )

    def _do_compile(self, key, signature, device, constexprs, global_constexprs, options, attrs):
        kernel_cache, _, target, _, _ = self.device_caches[device]

        src = self.ASTSource(self, signature, constexprs, attrs, global_constexprs)
        kernel = self.compile(src, target=target, options=options)
        kernel_cache[key] = kernel
        return kernel

    def __call__(self, *args, **kwargs):
        raise RuntimeError("Cannot call @substrate.jit'd outside of the scope of a kernel")


def jit(fn: Callable = None) -> Callable:
    def decorator(func: Callable) -> Callable:
        assert callable(func), "jit decorator must be used on a callable"
        return JITFunction(func)

    if fn is None:
        return decorator
    else:
        return decorator(fn)

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch
import substrate
import substrate.language as S


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shuffle_xor_i32(
    inp: S.Tensor((64,), S.i32),
    out: S.Tensor((64,), S.i32),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    out[tid] = S.shuffle_xor(inp[tid], 32, 64)


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shuffle_up_i32(
    inp: S.Tensor((64,), S.i32),
    out: S.Tensor((64,), S.i32),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    out[tid] = S.shuffle_up(inp[tid], 1, 64)


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shuffle_down_i32(
    inp: S.Tensor((64,), S.i32),
    out: S.Tensor((64,), S.i32),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    out[tid] = S.shuffle_down(inp[tid], 1, 64)


@substrate.jit
def kernel_shuffle_idx_i32(
    inp: S.Tensor((64,), S.i32),
    out: S.Tensor((64,), S.i32),
):
    tid = S.thread_id(0)
    out[tid] = S.shuffle(inp[tid], 32, 64)


class TestShuffle(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_shuffle_idx_i32(self):
        inp = torch.arange(64, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda") * 17 + 3
        out = torch.empty_like(inp)

        kernel_shuffle_idx_i32[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](inp, out)

        expected = torch.full((64,), inp[32].item(), dtype=torch.int32)
        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(out.cpu(), expected),
            f"Expected: {expected.tolist()}, Actual: {out.cpu().tolist()}",
        )

    def test_shuffle_up_i32(self):
        inp = torch.arange(64, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda") * 17 + 3
        out = torch.empty_like(inp)

        kernel_shuffle_up_i32[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](inp, out)

        expected = inp.cpu()[(torch.arange(64, dtype=torch.int64) - 1) % 64]
        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(out.cpu(), expected),
            f"Expected: {expected.tolist()}, Actual: {out.cpu().tolist()}",
        )

    def test_shuffle_down_i32(self):
        inp = torch.arange(64, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda") * 17 + 3
        out = torch.empty_like(inp)

        kernel_shuffle_down_i32[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](inp, out)

        expected = inp.cpu()[(torch.arange(64, dtype=torch.int64) + 1) % 64]
        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(out.cpu(), expected),
            f"Expected: {expected.tolist()}, Actual: {out.cpu().tolist()}",
        )

    def test_shuffle_xor_i32(self):
        inp = torch.arange(64, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda") * 17 + 3
        out = torch.empty_like(inp)

        kernel_shuffle_xor_i32[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](inp, out)

        expected = inp.cpu()[torch.arange(64, dtype=torch.int64) ^ 32]
        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(out.cpu(), expected),
            f"Expected: {expected.tolist()}, Actual: {out.cpu().tolist()}",
        )


if __name__ == "__main__":
    unittest.main()

import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import substrate
import substrate.language as S

def _launch():
    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))
INPUT0_SHAPE = (8, 64, 512, 1024)
OUTPUT_SHAPE = (8, 128, 510, 1022)
WEIGHT_SHAPE = (128, 64, 3, 3)

@substrate.jit
def fused_kernel(X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 1024), S.f32), W: S.Tensor((128, 64, 3, 3), S.f32), Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 510, 1022), S.f32)):
    for n in S.range(8):
        for oc in S.range(128):
            for o0 in S.range(510):
                for o1 in S.range(1022):
                    acc = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
                    g = oc // 128
                    ic_base = g * 64
                    for ic_local in S.range(64):
                        ic = ic_base + ic_local
                        for k0 in S.range(3):
                            for k1 in S.range(3):
                                i0 = o0 * 1 - 0 + k0 * 1
                                i1 = o1 * 1 - 0 + k1 * 1
                                if (i0 >= 0 and i0 < 512) and (i1 >= 0 and i1 < 1024):
                                    acc += S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.f32) * S.convert(W[oc, ic_local, k0, k1], S.f32)
                    Y[n, oc, o0, o1] = acc

class ModelNew(nn.Module):

    def __init__(self, in_channels: int, out_channels: int, kernel_size: int, stride: int = 1, padding: int = 0, dilation: int = 1, groups: int = 1, bias: bool = False):
            super(ModelNew, self).__init__()
            self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(in_channels, out_channels, (kernel_size, kernel_size), stride=stride, padding=padding, dilation=dilation, groups=groups, bias=bias)

    def forward(self, x):
        if tuple(x.shape) != (8, 64, 512, 1024) or x.dtype != torch.float32:
            raise RuntimeError('This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.')
        x0 = x.contiguous()
        w = self.conv2d.weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
        y = torch.empty((8, 128, 510, 1022), device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)
        fused_kernel[_launch](x0, w, y)
        return y

#!/usr/bin/env python3
import unittest

import torch

import substrate
import substrate.language as S
import _substrate_bindings as _C
from substrate.compiler.code_generator import (
    _build_import_module,
    _collect_jit_dependencies,
    _get_function_def,
)
from substrate.testing import has_rocm


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip(
    src: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    dst: S.Tensor((7,), S.i32),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)
    dst_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(dst, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    offset_x2 = S.convert(4, S.i32)
    offset_x4 = S.convert(12, S.i32)

    value_x1 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x1(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    value_x2 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x2(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    value_x4 = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)

    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x1(value_x1, dst_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x2(value_x2, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x2, 0)
    S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_store_x4(value_x4, dst_rsrc, zero, offset_x4, 0)


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view(
    src: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    dst: S.Tensor((8,), S.bf16),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    src_rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(src, range_bytes)

    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    packed = S.amdgpu.raw_buffer_load_x4(src_rsrc, zero, zero, 0)
    frag = S.view(packed, S.Tensor((2, 4, 1), S.bf16))

    for i in S.range(2):
        for j in S.range(4):
            dst[i * 4 + j] = frag[i, j, 0]


@substrate.jit
def kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_atomic_fadd(
    value: S.f32,
    buffer: S.Tensor((8,), S.f32),
    range_bytes: S.i32,
):
    rsrc = S.amdgpu.make_rsrc(buffer, range_bytes)
    zero = S.convert(0, S.i32)
    S.amdgpu.buffer_atomic_add_f32(value, rsrc, zero, zero, 0)


def generate_mlir(jit_fn) -> str:
    jit_deps = _collect_jit_dependencies(jit_fn)
    import_module = _build_import_module([jit_fn, *jit_deps])

    generator = _C.MLIRGenerator()
    generator.generate_from_python_ast(import_module)

    for dep in jit_deps:
        dep_func = _get_function_def(dep.parse())
        generator.visit_function_def(dep_func, "[]", "jit")

    kernel_func = _get_function_def(jit_fn.parse())
    generator.visit_function_def(kernel_func, "[]", "kernel")
    return generator.get_mlir()


@unittest.skipUnless(
    has_rocm(),
    "Requires ROCm/HIP with an AMD GPU.",
)
class TestAMDGPUBufferOps(unittest.TestCase):
    def test_raw_buffer_roundtrip(self):
        src = torch.arange(7, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda") * 17 - 9
        dst = torch.full((7,), -1, dtype=torch.int32, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_make_rsrc_generates_pointer_and_range(self):
        mlir = generate_mlir(kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_roundtrip)

        self.assertIn(
            "substrate.memref.extract_aligned_pointer_as_index",
            mlir,
        )
        self.assertGreaterEqual(mlir.count("vector.insert %arg2"), 2, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_load"), 3, mlir)
        self.assertEqual(mlir.count("substrate.gpu.amdgpu_raw_buffer_store"), 3, mlir)

    def test_raw_buffer_bf16_view_extract(self):
        src = torch.randn((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        dst = torch.zeros((8,), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = src.numel() * src.element_size()

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_bf16_view[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))](
            src, dst, range_bytes
        )

        self.assertTrue(
            torch.equal(dst.cpu(), src.cpu()),
            f"Expected: {src.tolist()}, Actual: {dst.tolist()}",
        )

    def test_raw_buffer_atomic_fadd(self):
        buffer = torch.zeros((8,), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
        range_bytes = buffer.numel() * buffer.element_size()

        # Each thread adds a different value to the same location
        value = torch.tensor(1.5, dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")

        kernel_amdgpu_raw_buffer_atomic_fadd[lambda: ((1, 8, 1), (1, 8, 1))](
            value, buffer, range_bytes
        )

        # All 8 threads added 1.5 to buffer[0], so result should be 12.0
        expected = 1.5 * 8
        self.assertAlmostEqual(

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    out = run_single((0, 0), (0, 0), b_all=True)
+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    out = run_single((0, 0), (0, 0), b_all=True)
+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    out = run_single((0, 0), (0, 0), b_all=True)
+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

+    tiles_n = (TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS + MFMA_N - 1) // MFMA_N
+    tile_m = bid // tiles_n
+    tile_n = bid - tile_m * tiles_n
+
+    oc_base = tile_m * MFMA_M
+    out_linear_base = tile_n * MFMA_N
+
+    lane_col = tid & 31
+    lane_half = tid // 32
+    lane_mod32 = tid - lane_half * 32
+
+    row_in_half = (lane_mod32 & 3) + ((lane_mod32 // 8) * 4)
+    mfma_row = row_in_half + lane_half * 16
+    k_inner_base = lane_half * 4
+
+    acc = S.make_local((MFMA_ACC,), S.f32)
+    a_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+    b_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+
+    for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        oc = oc_base + mfma_row
+        k_base = k_tile * MFMA_K + k_inner_base
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_idx = k_base + e
+            ic = k_idx // 9
+            k_rem = k_idx - ic * 9
+            k0 = k_rem // 3
+            k1 = k_rem - k0 * 3
+            a_frag[e] = S.convert(W[oc, ic, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+            if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+                n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+                out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+                o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+                i0 = o0 + k0
+                i1 = o1 + k1
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag, b_frag, acc)
+
+    out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+    if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+        n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+        out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+        o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+        o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+        for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+            Y[n, oc_base + lane_half * 16 + i, o0, o1] = acc[i]
+
 
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels: int,
+        out_channels: int,
+        kernel_size,
+        stride=1,
+        padding=0,
+        dilation=1,
+        groups: int = 1,
+        bias: bool = False,
+    ):
+        super().__init__()
+        if isinstance(kernel_size, int):
+            kernel_size = (kernel_size, kernel_size)
+        if isinstance(stride, int):
+            stride = (stride, stride)
+        if isinstance(padding, int):
+            padding = (padding, padding)
+        if isinstance(dilation, int):
+            dilation = (dilation, dilation)

-            self.conv2d = nn.Conv2d(in_channels, out_channels, (kernel_size, kernel_size), stride=stride, padding=padding, dilation=dilation, groups=groups, bias=bias)

+            in_channels,
+            out_channels,
+            kernel_size,
+            stride=stride,
+            padding=padding,
+            dilation=dilation,
+            groups=groups,
+            bias=bias,
+        )
+        self._cached_weight = None
+        self._cached_weight_key = None
 
+    def _get_prepared_weight(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight
+        key = (
+            x.device,
+            x.dtype,
+            weight.untyped_storage().data_ptr(),
+            weight._version,
+        )
+        if self._cached_weight_key != key:
+            self._cached_weight = weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_weight_key = key
+        return self._cached_weight
+
     def forward(self, x):
-        if tuple(x.shape) != (8, 64, 512, 1024) or x.dtype != torch.float32:
-            raise RuntimeError('This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.')
+        if tuple(x.shape) != INPUT0_SHAPE or x.dtype != torch.float32:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports the benchmark input shape and dtype.")
+        if self.conv2d.groups != 1:
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports groups=1.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.kernel_size) != (KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports a 3x3 kernel.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.stride) != (1, 1) or tuple(self.conv2d.padding) != (0, 0):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports stride=1 and padding=0.")
+        if tuple(self.conv2d.dilation) != (1, 1):
+            raise RuntimeError("This fused kernel only supports dilation=1.")
+
         x0 = x.contiguous()
-        w = self.conv2d.weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()

+        w = self._get_prepared_weight(x0)
+        y = torch.empty(OUTPUT_SHAPE, device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)
         fused_kernel[_launch](x0, w, y)
         return y

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    out = run_single((0, 0), (0, 0), b_all=True)
+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

+            k_idx = k_base + e
+            ic = k_idx // 9
+            k_rem = k_idx - ic * 9
+            k0 = k_rem // 3
+            k1 = k_rem - k0 * 3
+            a_frag[e] = S.convert(W[oc, ic, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+            if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+                n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+                out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+                o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+                i0 = o0 + k0
+                i1 = o1 + k1
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag, b_frag, acc)
+
+    out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+    if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+        n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+        out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+        o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+        o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+        for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+            Y[n, oc_base + lane_half * 16 + i, o0, o1] = acc[i]
+
 
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(
+        self,
+        in_channels: int,
+        out_channels: int,
+        kernel_size,
+        stride=1,
+        padding=0,
+        dilation=1,
+        groups: int = 1,
+        bias: bool = False,
+    ):

+            kernel_size = (kernel_size, kernel_size)
+        if isinstance(stride, int):
+            stride = (stride, stride)
+        if isinstance(padding, int):

+            weight.untyped_storage().data_ptr(),

+        )

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    out = run_single((0, 0), (0, 0), b_all=True)
+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor(INPUT0_SHAPE, S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor(WEIGHT_SHAPE, S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor(OUTPUT_SHAPE, S.f32),
+):

+    bid = S.block_id(0)
+
+    tiles_n = (TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS + MFMA_N - 1) // MFMA_N
+    tile_m = bid // tiles_n
+    tile_n = bid - tile_m * tiles_n
+

+    out_linear_base = tile_n * MFMA_N
+
+    lane_col = tid & 31
+    lane_half = tid // 32
+    lane_mod32 = tid - lane_half * 32
+
+    row_in_half = (lane_mod32 & 3) + ((lane_mod32 // 8) * 4)
+    mfma_row = row_in_half + lane_half * 16
+    k_inner_base = lane_half * 4
+
+    acc = S.make_local((MFMA_ACC,), S.f32)
+    a_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)

+
+    for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):

+

+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag, b_frag, acc)

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor(INPUT0_SHAPE, S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor(WEIGHT_SHAPE, S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor(OUTPUT_SHAPE, S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    bid = S.block_id(0)
+
+    tiles_n = (TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS + MFMA_N - 1) // MFMA_N
+    tile_m = bid // tiles_n
+    tile_n = bid - tile_m * tiles_n
+
+    oc_base = tile_m * MFMA_M
+    out_linear_base = tile_n * MFMA_N
+
+    lane_col = tid & 31
+    lane_half = tid // 32
+    lane_mod32 = tid - lane_half * 32
+
+    row_in_half = (lane_mod32 & 3) + ((lane_mod32 // 8) * 4)
+    mfma_row = row_in_half + lane_half * 16
+    k_inner_base = lane_half * 4
+
+    acc = S.make_local((MFMA_ACC,), S.f32)
+    a_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+    b_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+
+    for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        oc = oc_base + mfma_row
+        k_base = k_tile * MFMA_K + k_inner_base
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_idx = k_base + e
+            ic = k_idx // 9
+            k_rem = k_idx - ic * 9
+            k0 = k_rem // 3
+            k1 = k_rem - k0 * 3
+            a_frag[e] = S.convert(W[oc, ic, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+            if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+                n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+                out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+                o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+                i0 = o0 + k0
+                i1 = o1 + k1
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag, b_frag, acc)
+
+    out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+    if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+        n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+        out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+        o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+        o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+        for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+            Y[n, oc_base + lane_half * 16 + i, o0, o1] = acc[i]

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    out = run_single((0, 0), (0, 0), b_all=True)
+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    out = run_single((0, 0), (0, 0), b_all=True)
+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor(INPUT0_SHAPE, S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor(WEIGHT_SHAPE, S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor(OUTPUT_SHAPE, S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    bid = S.block_id(0)
+
+    tiles_n = (TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS + MFMA_N - 1) // MFMA_N
+    tile_m = bid // tiles_n
+    tile_n = bid - tile_m * tiles_n
+
+    oc_base = tile_m * MFMA_M
+    out_linear_base = tile_n * MFMA_N
+
+    lane_col = tid & 31
+    lane_half = tid // 32
+    lane_mod32 = tid - lane_half * 32
+
+    row_in_half = (lane_mod32 & 3) + ((lane_mod32 // 8) * 4)
+    mfma_row = row_in_half + lane_half * 16
+    k_inner_base = lane_half * 4
+
+    acc = S.make_local((MFMA_ACC,), S.f32)
+    a_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+    b_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+
+    for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        oc = oc_base + mfma_row
+        k_base = k_tile * MFMA_K + k_inner_base
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_idx = k_base + e
+            ic = k_idx // 9
+            k_rem = k_idx - ic * 9
+            k0 = k_rem // 3
+            k1 = k_rem - k0 * 3
+            a_frag[e] = S.convert(W[oc, ic, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+            if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+                n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+                out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+                o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+                i0 = o0 + k0
+                i1 = o1 + k1
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag, b_frag, acc)
+
+    out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+    if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+        n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+        out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+        o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+        o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+        for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+            Y[n, oc_base + lane_half * 16 + i, o0, o1] = acc[i]

 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S
 
+
+BATCH_SIZE = 8
+IN_CHANNELS = 64
+IN_H = 512
+IN_W = 1024
+OUT_CHANNELS = 128
+KERNEL_H = 3
+KERNEL_W = 3
+OUT_H = 510
+OUT_W = 1022
+
+INPUT0_SHAPE = (BATCH_SIZE, IN_CHANNELS, IN_H, IN_W)
+WEIGHT_SHAPE = (OUT_CHANNELS, IN_CHANNELS, KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)
+OUTPUT_SHAPE = (BATCH_SIZE, OUT_CHANNELS, OUT_H, OUT_W)
+
+MFMA_M = 32
+MFMA_N = 32
+MFMA_K = 8
+MFMA_ACC = 16
+OUT_PIXELS = OUT_H * OUT_W
+TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS = BATCH_SIZE * OUT_PIXELS
+K_TOTAL = IN_CHANNELS * KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W
+K_TILES = K_TOTAL // MFMA_K
+
+

-    return ((1, 1, 1), (1, 1, 1))

+    tiles_n = math.ceil(TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS / MFMA_N)
+    return ((tiles_m * tiles_n, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor(INPUT0_SHAPE, S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor(WEIGHT_SHAPE, S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor(OUTPUT_SHAPE, S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    bid = S.block_id(0)
+
+    tiles_n = (TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS + MFMA_N - 1) // MFMA_N
+    tile_m = bid // tiles_n
+    tile_n = bid - tile_m * tiles_n
+
+    oc_base = tile_m * MFMA_M
+    out_linear_base = tile_n * MFMA_N
+
+    lane_col = tid & 31
+    lane_half = tid // 32
+    lane_mod32 = tid - lane_half * 32
+
+    row_in_half = (lane_mod32 & 3) + ((lane_mod32 // 8) * 4)
+    mfma_row = row_in_half + lane_half * 16
+    k_inner_base = lane_half * 4
+
+    acc = S.make_local((MFMA_ACC,), S.f32)
+    a_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+    b_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+
+    for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        oc = oc_base + mfma_row
+        k_base = k_tile * MFMA_K + k_inner_base
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_idx = k_base + e
+            ic = k_idx // 9
+            k_rem = k_idx - ic * 9
+            k0 = k_rem // 3
+            k1 = k_rem - k0 * 3
+            a_frag[e] = S.convert(W[oc, ic, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+            if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+                n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+                out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+                o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+                i0 = o0 + k0
+                i1 = o1 + k1
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag, b_frag, acc)
+
+    out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+    if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+        n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+        out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+        o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+        o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+        for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+            Y[n, oc_base + lane_half * 16 + i, o0, o1] = acc[i]
+

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    out = run_single((0, 0), (0, 0), b_all=True)
+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    out = run_single((0, 0), (0, 0), b_all=True)
+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 1024), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((128, 64, 3, 3), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 510, 1022), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    bid = S.block_id(0)
+
+    tiles_n = (TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS + MFMA_N - 1) // MFMA_N
+    tile_m = bid // tiles_n
+    tile_n = bid - tile_m * tiles_n
+
+    oc_base = tile_m * MFMA_M
+    out_linear_base = tile_n * MFMA_N
+
+    lane_col = tid & 31
+    lane_half = tid // 32
+    lane_mod32 = tid - lane_half * 32
+
+    row_in_half = (lane_mod32 & 3) + ((lane_mod32 // 8) * 4)
+    mfma_row = row_in_half + lane_half * 16
+    k_inner_base = lane_half * 4
+
+    acc = S.make_local((MFMA_ACC,), S.f32)
+    a_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+    b_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+
+    for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):

+            k1 = k_rem - k0 * 3
+            a_frag[e] = S.convert(W[oc, ic, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col

+                i0 = o0 + k0
+                i1 = o1 + k1
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag, b_frag, acc)
+
+    out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+    if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+        n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+        out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+        o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+        o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+        for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()

+OUTPUT_SHAPE = (BATCH_SIZE, OUT_CHANNELS, OUT_H, OUT_W)
+
+MFMA_M = 32
+MFMA_N = 32
+MFMA_K = 8
+MFMA_ACC = 16
+OUT_PIXELS = OUT_H * OUT_W
+TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS = BATCH_SIZE * OUT_PIXELS
+K_TOTAL = IN_CHANNELS * KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W
+K_TILES = K_TOTAL // MFMA_K

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 1024), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((128, 64, 3, 3), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 510, 1022), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    bid = S.block_id(0)
+
+    tiles_n = (TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS + MFMA_N - 1) // MFMA_N
+    tile_m = bid // tiles_n
+    tile_n = bid - tile_m * tiles_n
+
+    oc_base = tile_m * MFMA_M
+    out_linear_base = tile_n * MFMA_N
+
+    lane_col = tid & 31
+    lane_half = tid // 32
+    lane_mod32 = tid - lane_half * 32
+
+    row_in_half = (lane_mod32 & 3) + ((lane_mod32 // 8) * 4)
+    mfma_row = row_in_half + lane_half * 16
+    k_inner_base = lane_half * 4
+
+    acc = S.make_local((MFMA_ACC,), S.f32)
+    a_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+    b_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+
+    for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        oc = oc_base + mfma_row
+        k_base = k_tile * MFMA_K + k_inner_base
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_idx = k_base + e
+            ic = k_idx // 9
+            k_rem = k_idx - ic * 9
+            k0 = k_rem // 3
+            k1 = k_rem - k0 * 3
+            a_frag[e] = S.convert(W[oc, ic, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+            if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+                n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+                out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+                o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+                i0 = o0 + k0
+                i1 = o1 + k1
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag, b_frag, acc)
+
+    out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+    if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+        n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+        out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+        o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+        o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+        for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+            Y[n, oc_base + lane_half * 16 + i, o0, o1] = acc[i]
+
 
 class ModelNew(nn.Module):
+    def __init__(

+        bias: bool = False,
+    ):

+            kernel_size = (kernel_size, kernel_size)
+        if isinstance(stride, int):
+            stride = (stride, stride)
+        if isinstance(padding, int):
+            padding = (padding, padding)
+        if isinstance(dilation, int):
+            dilation = (dilation, dilation)

+    def _get_prepared_weight(self, x: torch.Tensor) -> torch.Tensor:
+        weight = self.conv2d.weight

+            x.device,
+            x.dtype,
+            weight.untyped_storage().data_ptr(),

+        )

+            self._cached_weight = weight.to(device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype).contiguous()
+            self._cached_weight_key = key

     def forward(self, x):
-        if tuple(x.shape) != (8, 64, 512, 1024) or x.dtype != torch.float32:

+        y = torch.empty(OUTPUT_SHAPE, device=x.device, dtype=x.dtype)

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    out = run_single((0, 0), (0, 0), b_all=True)
+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    out = run_single((0, 0), (0, 0), b_all=True)
+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 1024), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((128, 64, 3, 3), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 510, 1022), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    bid = S.block_id(0)
+
+    tiles_n = (TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS + MFMA_N - 1) // MFMA_N
+    tile_m = bid // tiles_n
+    tile_n = bid - tile_m * tiles_n
+
+    oc_base = tile_m * MFMA_M
+    out_linear_base = tile_n * MFMA_N
+
+    lane_col = tid & 31
+    lane_half = tid // 32
+    lane_mod32 = tid - lane_half * 32
+
+    row_in_half = (lane_mod32 & 3) + ((lane_mod32 // 8) * 4)
+    mfma_row = row_in_half + lane_half * 16
+    k_inner_base = lane_half * 4
+
+    acc = S.make_local((MFMA_ACC,), S.f32)
+    a_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+    b_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+
+    for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        oc = oc_base + mfma_row
+        k_base = k_tile * MFMA_K + k_inner_base
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_idx = k_base + e
+            ic = k_idx // 9
+            k_rem = k_idx - ic * 9
+            k0 = k_rem // 3
+            k1 = k_rem - k0 * 3
+            a_frag[e] = S.convert(W[oc, ic, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+            if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+                n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+                out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+                o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+                i0 = o0 + k0
+                i1 = o1 + k1
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag, b_frag, acc)
+
+    out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+    if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+        n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+        out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+        o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+        o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+        for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+            Y[n, oc_base + lane_half * 16 + i, o0, o1] = acc[i]
+

import torch, importlib.util
path='/workspace/kernel_benchmark/kb_eval_pipeline/runs/kb1/p55/optimization_rounds_no_invariants/round1/mfma_probe_tmp.py'
spec=importlib.util.spec_from_file_location('probe', path)
mod=importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)
spec.loader.exec_module(mod)

def row_from_tid(tid):
    lane_mod32 = tid % 32
    lane_half = tid // 32
    return (lane_mod32 & 3) + ((lane_mod32 // 8) * 4) + lane_half * 16

def k_from_tid_elem(tid,e):
    return e + 4*(tid//32)

def simulate(a,b):
    A=torch.zeros((32,8),dtype=torch.float32)
    B=torch.zeros((8,32),dtype=torch.float32)
    for tid in range(64):
        r=row_from_tid(tid)
        c=tid%32
        for e in range(4):
            A[r,k_from_tid_elem(tid,e)] = float(a[tid,e])
            B[k_from_tid_elem(tid,e),c] = float(b[tid,e])
    C=A@B
    out=torch.zeros((64,16),dtype=torch.float32)
    for tid in range(64):
        c=tid%32
        half=tid//32
        for i in range(16):
            out[tid,i]=C[half*16+i,c]
    return out

a=torch.randn((64,4),dtype=torch.float32).to(torch.bfloat16).cuda()

out=out_gpu.cpu()

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 1024), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((128, 64, 3, 3), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 510, 1022), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    bid = S.block_id(0)
+
+    tiles_n = (TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS + MFMA_N - 1) // MFMA_N
+    tile_m = bid // tiles_n
+    tile_n = bid - tile_m * tiles_n
+
+    oc_base = tile_m * MFMA_M
+    out_linear_base = tile_n * MFMA_N
+
+    lane_col = tid & 31
+    lane_half = tid // 32
+    lane_mod32 = tid - lane_half * 32
+
+    row_in_half = (lane_mod32 & 3) + ((lane_mod32 // 8) * 4)
+    mfma_row = row_in_half + lane_half * 16
+    k_inner_base = lane_half * 4
+
+    acc = S.make_local((MFMA_ACC,), S.f32)
+    a_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+    b_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+
+    for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        oc = oc_base + mfma_row
+        k_base = k_tile * MFMA_K + k_inner_base
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_idx = k_base + e
+            ic = k_idx // 9
+            k_rem = k_idx - ic * 9
+            k0 = k_rem // 3
+            k1 = k_rem - k0 * 3
+            a_frag[e] = S.convert(W[oc, ic, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+            if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+                n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+                out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+                o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+                i0 = o0 + k0
+                i1 = o1 + k1
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag, b_frag, acc)
+
+    out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+    if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+        n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+        out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+        o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+        o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+        for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+            Y[n, oc_base + lane_half * 16 + i, o0, o1] = acc[i]
+

@@ -0,0 +1,42 @@
+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    out = run_single((0, 0), (0, 0), b_all=True)
+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    out = run_single((0, 0), (0, 0), b_all=True)
+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 1024), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((128, 64, 3, 3), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 510, 1022), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    bid = S.block_id(0)
+
+    tiles_n = (TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS + MFMA_N - 1) // MFMA_N
+    tile_m = bid // tiles_n
+    tile_n = bid - tile_m * tiles_n
+
+    oc_base = tile_m * MFMA_M
+    out_linear_base = tile_n * MFMA_N
+
+    lane_col = tid & 31
+    lane_half = tid // 32
+    lane_mod32 = tid - lane_half * 32
+
+    row_in_half = (lane_mod32 & 3) + ((lane_mod32 // 8) * 4)
+    mfma_row = row_in_half + lane_half * 16
+    k_inner_base = lane_half * 4
+
+    acc = S.make_local((MFMA_ACC,), S.f32)
+    a_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+    b_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+
+    for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        oc = oc_base + mfma_row
+        k_base = k_tile * MFMA_K + k_inner_base
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_idx = k_base + e
+            ic = k_idx // 9
+            k_rem = k_idx - ic * 9
+            k0 = k_rem // 3
+            k1 = k_rem - k0 * 3
+            a_frag[e] = S.convert(W[oc, ic, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+            if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+                n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+                out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+                o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+                i0 = o0 + k0
+                i1 = o1 + k1
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag, b_frag, acc)
+
+    out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+    if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+        n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+        out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+        o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+        o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+        for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+            Y[n, oc_base + lane_half * 16 + i, o0, o1] = acc[i]
+

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+

+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

 import torch.nn as nn
 import substrate
 import substrate.language as S
 
+
+BATCH_SIZE = 8
+IN_CHANNELS = 64
+IN_H = 512
+IN_W = 1024
+OUT_CHANNELS = 128
+KERNEL_H = 3
+KERNEL_W = 3
+OUT_H = 510
+OUT_W = 1022
+
+INPUT0_SHAPE = (BATCH_SIZE, IN_CHANNELS, IN_H, IN_W)
+WEIGHT_SHAPE = (OUT_CHANNELS, IN_CHANNELS, KERNEL_H, KERNEL_W)
+OUTPUT_SHAPE = (BATCH_SIZE, OUT_CHANNELS, OUT_H, OUT_W)
+
+MFMA_M = 32
+MFMA_N = 32
+MFMA_K = 8
+MFMA_ACC = 16
+OUT_PIXELS = OUT_H * OUT_W
+TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS = BATCH_SIZE * OUT_PIXELS
+K_TOTAL = IN_CHANNELS * KERNEL_H * KERNEL_W
+K_TILES = K_TOTAL // MFMA_K

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 1024), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((128, 64, 3, 3), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 510, 1022), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    bid = S.block_id(0)
+
+    tiles_n = (TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS + MFMA_N - 1) // MFMA_N
+    tile_m = bid // tiles_n
+    tile_n = bid - tile_m * tiles_n
+
+    oc_base = tile_m * MFMA_M
+    out_linear_base = tile_n * MFMA_N
+
+    lane_col = tid & 31
+    lane_half = tid // 32
+    lane_mod32 = tid - lane_half * 32
+
+    row_in_half = (lane_mod32 & 3) + ((lane_mod32 // 8) * 4)
+    mfma_row = row_in_half + lane_half * 16
+    k_inner_base = lane_half * 4
+
+    acc = S.make_local((MFMA_ACC,), S.f32)
+    a_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+    b_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+
+    for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        oc = oc_base + mfma_row
+        k_base = k_tile * MFMA_K + k_inner_base
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_idx = k_base + e
+            ic = k_idx // 9
+            k_rem = k_idx - ic * 9
+            k0 = k_rem // 3
+            k1 = k_rem - k0 * 3
+            a_frag[e] = S.convert(W[oc, ic, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+            if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+                n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+                out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+                o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+                i0 = o0 + k0
+                i1 = o1 + k1
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag, b_frag, acc)
+
+    out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+    if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+        n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+        out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+        o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+        o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+        for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+            Y[n, oc_base + lane_half * 16 + i, o0, o1] = acc[i]
+

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    out = run_single((0, 0), (0, 0), b_all=True)
+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

+import torch
+import substrate
+import substrate.language as S
+
+
+@substrate.jit
+def mfma_probe(
+    a: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    b: S.Tensor((64, 4), S.bf16),
+    out: S.Tensor((64, 16), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    acc = S.make_local((16,), S.f32)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+    acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a[tid], b[tid], acc)
+    for i in S.range(16):
+        out[tid, i] = acc[i]
+
+
+def run_single(a_idx, b_idx, b_all=False, a_all=False):
+    a = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    b = torch.zeros((64, 4), dtype=torch.bfloat16, device="cuda")
+    if a_all:
+        a[:] = 1
+    else:
+        a[a_idx] = 1
+    if b_all:
+        b[:] = 1
+    else:
+        b[b_idx] = 1
+    out = torch.empty((64, 16), dtype=torch.float32, device="cuda")
+    mfma_probe[lambda: ((1, 1, 1), (64, 1, 1))](a, b, out)
+    return out.cpu()
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    out = run_single((0, 0), (0, 0), b_all=True)
+    nz = torch.nonzero(out)
+    print("nonzero", nz.shape[0])
+    print(nz[:64])
+    print(out[nz[:16, 0], nz[:16, 1]])

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 1024), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((128, 64, 3, 3), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 510, 1022), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    bid = S.block_id(0)
+
+    tiles_n = (TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS + MFMA_N - 1) // MFMA_N
+    tile_m = bid // tiles_n
+    tile_n = bid - tile_m * tiles_n
+
+    oc_base = tile_m * MFMA_M
+    out_linear_base = tile_n * MFMA_N
+
+    lane_col = tid & 31
+    lane_half = tid // 32
+    lane_mod32 = tid - lane_half * 32
+
+    row_in_half = (lane_mod32 & 3) + ((lane_mod32 // 8) * 4)
+    mfma_row = row_in_half + lane_half * 16
+    k_inner_base = lane_half * 4
+
+    acc = S.make_local((MFMA_ACC,), S.f32)
+    a_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+    b_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+
+    for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        oc = oc_base + mfma_row
+        k_base = k_tile * MFMA_K + k_inner_base
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_idx = k_base + e
+            ic = k_idx // 9
+            k_rem = k_idx - ic * 9
+            k0 = k_rem // 3
+            k1 = k_rem - k0 * 3
+            a_frag[e] = S.convert(W[oc, ic, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+            if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+                n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+                out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+                o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+                i0 = o0 + k0
+                i1 = o1 + k1
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag, b_frag, acc)
+
+    out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+    if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+        n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+        out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+        o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+        o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+        for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+            Y[n, oc_base + lane_half * 16 + i, o0, o1] = acc[i]

+def fused_kernel(
+    X: S.Tensor((8, 64, 512, 1024), S.f32),
+    W: S.Tensor((128, 64, 3, 3), S.f32),
+    Y: S.Tensor((8, 128, 510, 1022), S.f32),
+):
+    tid = S.thread_id(0)
+    bid = S.block_id(0)
+
+    tiles_n = (TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS + MFMA_N - 1) // MFMA_N
+    tile_m = bid // tiles_n
+    tile_n = bid - tile_m * tiles_n
+
+    oc_base = tile_m * MFMA_M
+    out_linear_base = tile_n * MFMA_N
+
+    lane_col = tid & 31
+    lane_half = tid // 32
+    lane_mod32 = tid - lane_half * 32
+
+    row_in_half = (lane_mod32 & 3) + ((lane_mod32 // 8) * 4)
+    mfma_row = row_in_half + lane_half * 16
+    k_inner_base = lane_half * 4
+
+    acc = S.make_local((MFMA_ACC,), S.f32)
+    a_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+    b_frag = S.make_local((4,), S.bf16)
+
+    for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+        acc[i] = S.convert(0.0, S.f32)
+
+    for k_tile in S.range(K_TILES):
+        oc = oc_base + mfma_row
+        k_base = k_tile * MFMA_K + k_inner_base
+
+        for e in S.range(4):
+            k_idx = k_base + e
+            ic = k_idx // 9
+            k_rem = k_idx - ic * 9
+            k0 = k_rem // 3
+            k1 = k_rem - k0 * 3
+            a_frag[e] = S.convert(W[oc, ic, k0, k1], S.bf16)
+
+            out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+            if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+                n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+                out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+                o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+                o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+                i0 = o0 + k0
+                i1 = o1 + k1
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(X[n, ic, i0, i1], S.bf16)
+            else:
+                b_frag[e] = S.convert(0.0, S.bf16)
+
+        acc = S.amdgpu.mfma_32x32x8_bf16_f32(a_frag, b_frag, acc)
+
+    out_linear = out_linear_base + lane_col
+    if out_linear < TOTAL_OUTPUT_POSITIONS:
+        n = out_linear // OUT_PIXELS
+        out_rem = out_linear - n * OUT_PIXELS
+        o0 = out_rem // OUT_W
+        o1 = out_rem - o0 * OUT_W
+        for i in S.range(MFMA_ACC):
+            Y[n, oc_base + lane_half * 16 + i, o0, o1] = acc[i]
+
